
============== high level task decomposition ================
[{'objective': 'Express the product in terms of a polynomial evaluated at the 13th roots of unity and simplify it using factorization properties.'}, {'objective': 'Evaluate the simplified polynomial expression or product explicitly using known identities related to roots of unity.'}, {'objective': 'Calculate the numerical value of the simplified product.'}, {'objective': 'Find the remainder when the calculated product is divided by 1000.'}]
============== task analysis ================
1. Extract and Summarize Given Information:
- The problem involves the 13th roots of unity, denoted by \( \omega \), where \( \omega^{13} = 1 \) and \( \omega \neq 1 \).
- The product is taken over \( k = 0 \) to \( 12 \), i.e., over all 13th roots of unity including 1 (since \( \omega^0 = 1 \)).
- The expression inside the product is \( 2 - 2\omega^k + \omega^{2k} \).

2. Analyze Relationships Between Components:
- The 13th roots of unity satisfy the equation \( x^{13} - 1 = 0 \).
- The product involves evaluating a quadratic polynomial in \( \omega^k \) for each root.
- Since the roots are complex numbers on the unit circle, powers \( \omega^k \) cycle through all roots.
- The product over all roots of unity of a polynomial evaluated at these roots often relates to the resultant or factorization of polynomials.
- The inclusion of \( k=0 \) (i.e., \( \omega^0 = 1 \)) means the product includes the factor evaluated at 1.
- The polynomial inside the product can be rewritten or factored to understand its roots or to relate it to cyclotomic polynomials.

3. Identify the Field of Study:
- The problem lies primarily in algebra and number theory.
- Specifically, it involves complex roots of unity, cyclotomic polynomials, and modular arithmetic.
- Subfields include algebraic number theory and polynomial factorization.
- Such problems commonly appear in mathematical competitions and in the study of discrete Fourier transforms or algebraic integers.

4. Highlight Aspects Needing Clarification:
- The problem is clear in its statement; however, the expression inside the product might be simplified or transformed for easier analysis.
- Potential challenges include handling complex roots and simplifying the product without direct computation.
- Understanding how to reduce the product modulo 1000 requires insight into the algebraic structure or numeric properties.
- No ambiguity in the problem statement, but the complexity lies in the algebraic manipulation and modular arithmetic.

    from collections import Counter
    print("Task Requirement: ", taskInfo)
    sub_tasks = []
    agents = []
    logs = []

    cot_sc_instruction_1 = "Sub-task 1: Rewrite and simplify the expression inside the product, i.e., transform 2 - 2*omega^k + omega^(2k) into a more tractable polynomial form or factorization to facilitate evaluation over roots of unity, with context from the user query."
    N = self.max_sc
    cot_agents_1 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.5) for _ in range(N)]

        "subtask_id": "subtask_1",
        "instruction": cot_sc_instruction_1,

    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 1 output: thinking - {thinking1.content}; answer - {answer1.content}")

    subtask_desc_5 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_5",
        "instruction": reflect_instruction_5,
        "context": ["user query", thinking4c.content, answer4c.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "Reflexion"
    }
    thinking5, answer5 = await cot_agent_5(cot_inputs_5, reflect_instruction_5, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_5.id}, reducing modulo 1000, thinking: {thinking5.content}; answer: {answer5.content}")
    for i in range(N_max_5):
        feedback, correct = await critic_agent_5([taskInfo, thinking5, answer5], 
                                                "Please review the answer above and criticize on where might be wrong. If you are absolutely sure it is correct, output exactly 'True' in 'correct'", 
                                                i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {critic_agent_5.id}, providing feedback, thinking: {feedback.content}; answer: {correct.content}")
        if correct.content.strip() == "True":
            break
        cot_inputs_5.extend([thinking5, answer5, feedback])
        thinking5, answer5 = await cot_agent_5(cot_inputs_5, reflect_instruction_5, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_5.id}, refining modulo reduction, thinking: {thinking5.content}; answer: {answer5.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 5 output: thinking - {thinking5.content}; answer - {answer5.content}")
    subtask_desc_5['response'] = {"thinking": thinking5, "answer": answer5}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_5)
    print("Step 5: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    final_answer = await self.make_final_answer(thinking5, answer5, sub_tasks, agents)
    return final_answer, logs
